74.20(1): 'tsho byed sman pa'i rgyal po chen po lags/ yan lag sngo sbyor sde ru gsungs pa ni/
74.21(1): bdag cag 'khor rnams kun la bshad du gsol/ de skad zhus te ston pas bka' 
75.1(1): stsal pa/ dpyad bu la sogs nyan pa'i 'khor rnams nyon/ yan lag gsum pa sngo yi 
75.2(1): sbyor ba 'di/ mtha' 'khob gnas su skyes pa'i sman pa la/ yul du sman med thag 
75.3(1): ring sman mi rnyed/ nad la sman yig klog pas ga na phan/ dper na go mtshon med 
75.4(1): pa'i dpa' bo 'dra/ mtha' 'khob sman pa sman pa'i yi dwags yin/ gal te bzang 
75.5(1): drug la sogs thag ring bzang sman rnams/ dbul po nor med rnams kyis mi khug 
75.6(1): cing / sman mod byams sems chung bas nor ngo byed/ dbul po'i nad la bzang 
75.7(1): drug khos mi 'debs/ nor med dbul po'i nad pa kun don du/ mtha' 'khob sman 
75.8(1): pa kun gyi don ched du/ snang tshad rtsi shing sman du ston par byed/ 'phral du btus 
75.9(1): pas nus pa ma yal pas/ thug 'phrad nad gsod me la chu blug 'dra/ yun ring sman 
75.10(1): gyi nus sang rno med pa/ thag ring 'ong ba'i bzang sman kun las 'phags/ rtsi shing 
75.11(1): sngo mi skye ba'i yul med pas/ zad med rin po che'i gter dang 'dra/ 'di la don 
75.12(1): ched rnam pa bdun yin te/ skye sa btu lugs dug 'don skam lugs dang / spang 
75.13(1): blang 'jam sdeb sbyor te sde bdun bstan/ sngo sbyor 'di yi man ngag gces pa yin/
75.14(1): dang po skyes sa ri rgyal gtsang ma ste/ gangs brag byin chen bkra shis nyams dga' 
75.15(1): ba/ bsil drod snyom dang grub thob zhabs kyis bcag /nyi zla'i mdangs len sa gzhi 
75.16(1): gshin par btu/ gnyis pa btu dus lo 'bras rtsa ba ni/ dus tshad gsum la btu ba 
75.17(1): man ngag ste/ dang po rus nad rmang pa gsal byed sdong po yin/ rtsi skam rtsa ba nus 
75.18(1): pa 'dus pas ston kha'am/ yang na lo ma 'bus kha dpyid dus btu/ rtsa rgyud sha yi 
75.19(1): nad rnams lo mas sel/ lo rgyas rgan du ma song dbyar dus btu/ don snod mgo 
75.20(1): bo'i nad rnams 'bras bus sel/ rtsi rgyas sad kyis ma khyer ston kha btu/ lpags 
75.21(1): pa nang grol lto nad shun pas sel/ me tog kha 'bus dbyar dpyid mtshams su 
76.1(1): btu/ bshal sman nus pa gting 'gro ston dgun mtshams/ skyug sman nus pa gyen rgyu 
76.2(1): dgun dpyid mtshams/ brtson 'grus ldan pa'i rtsol bas btu ba ste/ khyad par zla ba 
76.3(1): yar ngo'i dus bzang la/ gtsang ma'i bu tsha bu mo khrus byas nas/ kha nas sman 'dzab 
76.4(1): brjod cing gyen 'gro nas/ rtsa ba btu nas yal ga ldong po bcas/ lo ma'i bcud 
76.5(1): la zho dang myu gu bcas/ me tog 'bras bu btu na rtse mo btu/ shun pa bar shun tshil 
76.6(1): dang bcas pa kun/ snying po rtsi dang nus pa yin pas na/ 'bong ma bzhin du lhag 
76.7(1): ma med par btu/ gsum pa dug yod bcad par bya ba ni/ rtsa ba rkang dug sdong po 
76.8(1): tshigs pa'i dug /yal ga lo ma'i dug la me tog gos kyi dug /'bras bu rus dug 
76.9(1): zho rkang tshil gyi dug /kog pa lpags dug shun pa sha yi dug /nang shun sha gdan 
76.10(1): dug tu yod pa ni/ dper na rin chen g.ya' dang phral na gsal ba bzhin/ dug 
76.11(1): phral sman ni 'jam zhing zhu rjes bzang / ngad phral skam legs 'jam sbyor mkhas pa 
76.12(1): dgos/ bzhi pa skam lugs de ltar btus pa'i sman/ bsil gyi sman rnams grib ma 
76.13(1): lhag pas skam/ drod kyi sman rnams me dang nyi mar skam/ rul sum ma shor ma nyams 
76.14(1): ma tshig pa/ sme mnol ma song dud bas ma bzung pa/ ro dang nus pa ldan pas yon 
76.15(1): tan che/ lnga pa spang dang blang tshul ldan pa ni/ sngo sman yin pas nus pa yal sla bas/
76.16(1): lo re bzhin du gsar btsal rnying pa 'pho/ drug pa 'jam sdeb 'di la gsum yod ste/
76.17(1): sbyor ba kha 'dzin 'jam dang gnyen po gsum/ dang po sbyor ba 'jam btsal sdeb pa 
76.18(1): ni/ tsha grang rigs mthun so sor mang sdeb pas/ rtsub pa'i rigs rnams 'jam pas 
76.19(1): zhi ba yin/ gnyis pa kha 'dzin 'jam btsal gsum yod ste/ pho ba'i sman rnams 
76.20(1): se 'bru sdeb na 'jam/ don la bzang drug snod la pi pi ling / gang la gtong ba'i 
76.21(1): sngo sman de dang sdeb/ kha 'dzin de'i cha yis 'jam pa yin/ gsum pa gnyen po'i 
77.1(1): 'jam sdeb ma mkhas na/ sngo sman rnams la zur rtsub gcan khyi 'dra/ rlung bskyed 
77.2(1): pho ba'i drod gsod lus zung skem/ dper na rlung shas can la bu ram bsdebs/ pho 
77.3(1): ba'i drod gso se 'bru sman nag dang / lus zung bskyed byed a ru gser mdog 
77.4(1): gsum/ de rnams bsdeb na khan d+ha byas na mchog /phye ma 'am ni lag len gang 
77.5(1): bder spyod/ bdun pa sbyor sde 'di la rnam pa gnyis yod de/ tsha sel grang sel rnam 
77.6(1): pa gnyis yin te/ bsil drod ma 'dres 'jam sbyor mthun sdeb nas/ ro dang nus 
77.7(1): pa zhu rjes mthun par sbyar/ dang po tsha sel 'di la rnam pa gnyis yin te/ thun 
77.8(1): mongs spyi 'jom kha bsgyur gang 'gro la/ dang po thun mongs rje blon drug pa ni/ rgyal 
77.9(1): po zla bsil g.ya' skyes nag po ni/ tshad pa mkhris pa 'joms pa'i bdud rtsi yin/
77.10(1): btsun mo re skon khrag tshad bya ra byed/ sras bu sro lo 'jib rtsis mchin nad gnon/
77.11(1): blon po sgong tog par pa ta yis 'khrug tshad sel/ dmag dpon tig ta spang rtsi yis/
77.12(1): tsha ba gsar rnying gang yang 'joms shing gsod/ hong len ba sha kha ni 'bangs yin 
77.13(1): te/ dpon blon sdong byed don tshad ma lus sel/ blon 'bangs drug gis tsha rims 
77.14(1): kha bsgyur phyir/ thun log bsdus la dmag mi thun re ste/ dmag mi bsil ba'i sngo 
77.15(1): sman gang 'dus sbyar/ 'di rnams mgyogs pa gang chu rta yis phul/ gab tshad so ma 
77.16(1): yin na gdus thang btang / rgyas tshad yin na gdus thang bskol grang byas la btang /
77.17(1): stongs tshad 'bring po'i chang dang sbyar/ rnying tshad yin na bskos grang byas nas 
77.18(1): btang / gnyis pa kha sgyur sngo sbyor bdun pa ni/ dang po gtso bo gzhi bzung sman bzhi 
77.19(1): ni/ 'khrug tshad don tshad sel byed hong len dang / dug tshad rnying tshad sel byed 
77.20(1): spang rtsi re skon pa/ rtsa tshad khrag tshad sel byed khyi lce ba/ rgyal po bzhi yin thun log 
77.21(1): gnyis ltabs bsdu/ blon po spun mang kha sgyur nyer gcig ni/ rnam par khrag rkang 
78.1(1): 'bam po myu gu shing / bsten na yan lag chu 'thung tshad pa gcod/ rgu drus spang 
78.2(1): tshan sbu ru dar ya kan/ khrag skam rtsa mthud byang khog tshad pa sel/ stag sha phur 
78.3(1): thal mgron bu'i thal ba yis/ khog stod rnag khrag chu ser skem par byed/ a byag sro 
78.4(1): lo stab seng mgo chag gso/ pus dkar lug chung khur rtsas smug po sel/ a byag 
78.5(1): dug pus ra dug gnyan gzer 'joms/ gcig thub stag sha 'dza' yas (ming can )
78.6(1): gag lhog 'joms/ g.yer shing btsod dang sran mas 'brum nag sel/ btsod 
78.7(1): dang bong nga gang chung tshad 'khru sel/ sgang thog bye'u 'om bus sha dug sel/ bong 
78.8(1): nga dkar dang ha bo re ral sbyar dug sel/ sro lo sgang thog bong ba dkar pos tshad 
78.9(1): mkhris 'joms/ stab seng rta pags ri 'tshos 'grams tshad sel/ spang rtsi sngo sprin skra 
78.10(1): bzang rims tshad sel/ btsod dang 'bri mog lug chung khrag tshad sel/ rtswa mkhris 
78.11(1): bong nga skyer pas mkhris tshad sel/ snya lo khur rtsa 'jib rtsis pho tshad sel/ snya lo 
78.12(1): bong nga btsod kyis rgyu tshad sel/ / yung ba de ba skyer shun sha tshad sel/ lug ru brag 
78.13(1): spos snyi bas rtsa tshad sel/ stab seng se rgod gang chung rus tshad sel/ mtshan dkar 
78.14(1): snyi ba rgod spos snying tshad sel/ sro lo sug 'dra spang rgyan glo tshad sel/ rtsi'u sum cu 
78.15(1): tig mtshal mchin tshad sel/ rgod spos byi tsher khrag rkang mtsher tshad sel/ shug 
78.16(1): tsher byi tsher nyi dgas mkhal tshad sel/ stab seng rta lpags ri tshos 'gram tshad sel/
78.17(1): sro lo sgang thog bong ngas 'khrug tshad 'jom/ bong nga a bo re ral sbyar dug 'jom/
78.18(1): 'om bu sgang thog byi'us sha dug 'joms/ gang ga chung btsod bong ngas 'khrug tshad 
78.19(1): 'joms/ sran ma g.yer shing btsod kyis 'brum nag sel/ se rgod skyer shun lpags 
78.20(1): 'brum chu ser sel/ rgyal po bzhi ni rtsa ba gzhi ma la/ thang dang phye ma gang byed blon 
78.21(1): pos bsgyur/ pho ba'i me drod che na phye la byed/ pho bas zas 'dul chung ba thang byas 
79.1(1): chog /phye ma byed na ka ras kha blang gces/ gnyis pa grang sel sngo sman bcu bzhi ni/
79.2(1): rgyal po cong zhi rgod btul gzhir bzung nas/ de la li sug sgog 'dzim pi pi ling /
79.3(1): de yi kha bsgyur pho ba'i me drod bskyed/ sran ma phab dang bul tog tsam pa 'ju / lce 
79.4(1): tsha za 'bras 'jib bus ma zhu 'ju / zel tsha srub kha go thal skran 'gril bshigs/ bre 
79.5(1): ga rgod trang rtse'us glo nad sel/ lca ba ra mnye ba spus skya rbab 'joms/ lce cha srub 
79.6(1): kha mgron bus dmu rdzing skem/ mdze tshwa ba spru pa yag mngal 'bras bshig /ze tshwa byi 
79.7(1): zung ba spus grang skran bshig /se rgod 'jib rtsi drod sman mchin nad sel/ lca ba 
79.8(1): dbyi mang ba sprus mkhal nad sel/ gze ma spa 'brum ra mnyes chu ser sel/ ra mnye 
79.9(1): nyer shing sha rus grang ba gcod/ kun la bur dkar chu bskol rta sbyar phul/ gzhan 
79.10(1): yang nyer shing ra mnye ba spu dang / lca ba la phud cong lgag drug /da lis srub ka dbyi 
79.11(1): mang lce tsha za lo lo ma lnga/ star bu gze ma lcam pa thang phrom bzhi'i 'bras bu bzhi/ ra 
79.12(1): dug pa'i me tog rgyas dus me tog gcig /lan tshwa bul tshwa ze tshwa tsha ba gsum/ rdo 
79.13(1): thal go brun gnyis la thal ba gnyis/ bu ram rta la chu tshan phul byas nas/ grang 
79.14(1): ba'i nad rigs kun la rtsi ru che/ grang sel spyi 'jom bco lnga pa de zhes/ tsha grang 
79.15(1): gnyis ka bsdom pa'i sngo sman la/ spyi yi sbyor sde sum cu rtsa drug yod/ de ltar rtsa ba 
79.16(1): lnga dang yan lag bzhi ste dgu/ 'du ba 'joms pa zhi byed sde yin la/ dpyad bu la 
79.17(1): sogs 'khor rnams kun gyis zungs/ ces gsungs te gso ba sman 'bum dkar po 
79.18(1): las/ sngo sman gyi sbyor sde bstan pa'i le'u ste bcu gnyis pa'o// //
79.19(1): 7 de nas yang gso ba rig pa 'dzin pa'i dpyad bu khri shes kyis gsol pa/ kyai 
79.20(1): 'tsho mdzad sman pa'i rgyal po chen po lags/ log non rin po che'i sbyor ba gsungs 
79.21(1): pa de/ bdag cag 'khor rnams kun la bshad du gsol/ de skad zhus pas ston 
80.1(1): pas bka' stsal pa/ dpyad bu la sogs 'khor rnams nges par nyon/ rtsa ba yan 
80.2(1): lag yang yang bsdeb pa de/ nad la tshod shor sman 'dred nad ma thon/ de rnams 
80.3(1): kun gyi log non rin po che/ byang khog mgo dang yan lag nad rnams la/ bad rlung 
80.4(1): khrag mkhris dmu 'or mdze 'bras dang / gag lhog gnyan dang sa bdag klu gnyan 
80.5(1): rgyal po'i nad/ bzhi brgya rtsa bzhi'i nad rnams 'di yis sel/ nad med yin na 
80.6(1): bcud len 'gog tu 'gro/ des na rin chen sbyor ba 'di ni spyi 'jom mchog /'di 
80.7(1): la tsha sbyor grang sbyor gnyis yod ste/ rin chen tsha sbyor gser dngul zangs lcags 
80.8(1): bzhi/ sbrang gshog tsam brdung sen mos dum bur gtub/ zhig dka'i rkang bur 
80.9(1): blug ste dngul chu blug /tshwa la mu zi blug ste steng nas mnan/ de'i steng du lci phye dam 
80.10(1): du bsdig /'dam pas kha bcad rlangs pa 'bud mi bya/ sol ba'i mes bsregs 
80.11(1): mu zi yal yal bsreg /thal ba mu zi gu khul sro ma ra/ chu dag tsi tra ka dang tsha ba 
80.12(1): gsum/ re skon seng ldeng mgron thal zhib par btag /dngul chu zho phyed star bu zho 
80.13(1): gcig bshig /a ru chang sbangs khu ba khan d+ha gdus/ gong ma rnams dang bsdus 
80.14(1): la ril lu sran ma tsam/ tho rangs lnga bdun dgu bskyed chang gis phul/ dreg dang 
80.15(1): grum bu sur ya mdze 'bras dang / rtsa nad tsha skran dmu 'or rnag chu skem/ gnyis pa 
80.16(1): rin chen grang sbyor sde tshan bstan pa ni/ bsten thabs sbyor ba log gnon gsum 
80.17(1): yin te/ dang po bsten thabs g.ya' phyi dug 'don dang / 'jam btsal sna khrid 
80.18(1): bshig dang rtsa kha dbye/ snod gtong phyi bsrung nus pa bskyed pa ste/ dang po g.ya' 
80.19(1): la sman ni tsha ba gsum dang dngul chu gnyis/ lhes ge'i nang du g.ya' ma thon bar 
80.20(1): mnye/ de rjes ba chur btag la g.ya' dug 'don/ gnyis pa dug 'don cong zhi dri 
80.21(1): chus skem skem btso/ gsum pa 'jam btsal pi pi ling dang pho ba ris/ nag mtshur

81.2(1): dang bstun nas tshad ldan sbyar/ bzhi pa sna khrid chang dang dbyi mang btang / dkar 
81.3(1): po gnyis sbyar btang bas nad thog ril lu gyur/ tsha ba'i nad la sna khrid chu yis

81.13(1): thal a ru ra/ sug sme gser gyi bye ma byang sems gnyis/ kun dang star bu bsnyam te
